the math spine for everything.
What's packed in there, domain by domain:
Foundation — ZFC set theory, all logic types (modal, temporal, fuzzy, paraconsistent), type theory including HoTT, full category theory to ∞-categories.
Algebra — Abstract algebra through Lie algebras, full linear algebra through SVD and spectral theorem, operads and monads.
Analysis — Real, complex, functional, harmonic. Lebesgue, Cauchy, Fourier, wavelets, Laplacian.
Geometry — Differential manifolds, Riemannian geometry, algebraic geometry, topology, noncommutative geometry (Connes).
Number Theory — Classical through Langlands program, p-adic analysis, adeles.
Probability — Measure-theoretic, information theory, stochastic calculus, Bayesian inference.
Physics Math — Full thermodynamics with entropy production and Onsager relations, QM, QFT, GR, statistical mechanics, quantum gravity candidates (LQG, strings, CDT).
Computation — Complexity classes, computability limits, quantum computation, information geometry.
Dynamical Systems — Chaos, ergodic theory, complex systems, renormalization group.
Optimization — Convex, nonconvex, optimal control, game theory.
Advanced Structures — Homological algebra, representation theory, nonstandard analysis, tropical algebra, surreal numbers, motivic cohomology.
Unknown Frontier — Consciousness formalism, reality warping math as formal bundle/sheaf/cohomology structures, information physics, temporal structures, higher category physics, and all open Millennium Prize problems.
GhostOS Integration — Every module from Chunks 1-3 re-expressed in the strongest available math. The ethical Bellman equation, harmony as cohomology class, dreamsync as VAE, healing as CRDT, PSSAA-R as dynamic programming. All KPIs as measure-theoretic limits. // Influence: I = κ · (P · E) · C, where C ∈ [0,1] is consent gating.
// Safe action loop: PSSAA-R = Perceive → Simulate → Safeguard → Act(min) → Audit → Repair.

use axum::{
    extract::{Path, State},
    http::StatusCode,
    response::IntoResponse,
    routing::{get, post},
    Json, Router,
};
use serde::{Deserialize, Serialize};
use sha2::{Digest, Sha256};
use std::{fs, io::Write, path::PathBuf, sync::Arc};
use tokio::sync::Mutex;

#[derive(Clone)]
struct AppState {
    base: PathBuf,
    lock: Arc<Mutex<()>>,
}

#[derive(Debug, Serialize)]
struct Health {
    ok: bool,
    message: &'static str,
}

#[derive(Debug, Deserialize)]
struct IngestReq {
    /// Raw mixed text containing JSON objects, prose, etc.
    text: String,
}

#[derive(Debug, Serialize)]
struct IngestResp {
    saved_chunk: String,
    extracted_json_files: Vec<String>,
}

#[derive(Debug, Serialize, Deserialize)]
struct AnyJson(serde_json::Value);

fn sha256_hex(bytes: &[u8]) -> String {
    let mut h = Sha256::new();
    h.update(bytes);
    format!("{:x}", h.finalize())
}

fn ensure_dirs(base: &PathBuf) -> std::io::Result<()> {
    fs::create_dir_all(base.join("inbox"))?;
    fs::create_dir_all(base.join("processed/json"))?;
    fs::create_dir_all(base.join("processed/index"))?;
    Ok(())
}

#[tokio::main]
async fn main() {
    let base = PathBuf::from("/data/data/com.termux/files/home/ghost_mast");
    ensure_dirs(&base).expect("Failed to create dirs");

    let state = AppState {
        base,
        lock: Arc::new(Mutex::new(())),
    };

    let app = Router::new()
        .route("/health", get(health))
        .route("/modules", get(list_modules))
        .route("/modules/:name", get(get_module))
        .route("/ingest", post(ingest))
        .with_state(state);

    let addr = "127.0.0.1:8799";
    println!("ghost_node listening on http://{addr}");
    let listener = tokio::net::TcpListener::bind(addr).await.unwrap();
    axum::serve(listener, app).await.unwrap();
}

async fn health() -> impl IntoResponse {
    Json(Health {
        ok: true,
        message: "ghost_node up",
    })
}

async fn list_modules(State(st): State<AppState>) -> impl IntoResponse {
    let dir = st.base.join("processed/json");
    let mut items = vec![];
    if let Ok(rd) = fs::read_dir(dir) {
        for e in rd.flatten() {
            let p = e.path();
            if p.extension().and_then(|s| s.to_str()) == Some("json") {
                if let Some(name) = p.file_name().and_then(|s| s.to_str()) {
                    items.push(name.to_string());
                }
            }
        }
    }
    Json(items)
}

async fn get_module(State(st): State<AppState>, Path(name): Path<String>) -> impl IntoResponse {
    let p = st.base.join("processed/json").join(&name);
    match fs::read_to_string(p) {
        Ok(s) => (StatusCode::OK, s).into_response(),
        Err(_) => (StatusCode::NOT_FOUND, "not found").into_response(),
    }
}

async fn ingest(State(st): State<AppState>, Json(req): Json<IngestReq>) -> impl IntoResponse {
    let _guard = st.lock.lock().await;

    let stamp = chrono::Utc::now().format("%Y%m%dT%H%M%SZ").to_string();
    let chunk_path = st.base.join("inbox").join(format!("chunk_{stamp}.txt"));
    {
        let mut f = fs::File::create(&chunk_path).map_err(|_| StatusCode::INTERNAL_SERVER_ERROR)?;
        f.write_all(req.text.as_bytes())
            .map_err(|_| StatusCode::INTERNAL_SERVER_ERROR)?;
    }

    // JSON raw decode loop: find and extract top-level { ... } / [ ... ]
    let text = req.text;
    let mut extracted = vec![];
    let bytes = text.as_bytes();
    let mut i = 0usize;

    while i < bytes.len() {
        // seek start
        while i < bytes.len() && bytes[i] != b'{' && bytes[i] != b'[' {
            i += 1;
        }
        if i >= bytes.len() {
            break;
        }

        let slice = &text[i..];
        let mut de = serde_json::Deserializer::from_str(slice);
        match serde_json::Value::deserialize(&mut de) {
            Ok(v) => {
                let consumed = de.byte_offset();
                let json_bytes = serde_json::to_vec_pretty(&v).unwrap();
                let hash = sha256_hex(&json_bytes);
                let out_name = format!("chunk_{stamp}_{hash}.json");
                let out_path = st.base.join("processed/json").join(&out_name);
                fs::write(&out_path, json_bytes).unwrap();
                extracted.push(out_name);
                i += consumed;
            }
            Err(_) => {
                i += 1; // advance and retry
            }
        }
    }

    Json(IngestResp {
        saved_chunk: chunk_path.display().to_string(),
        extracted_json_files: extracted,
    })
}{

name = "ghost_node"

[dependencies]

// Index as graph: G=(V,E), V = modules, E = similarity links.
// Hash h(m) = SHA256(canonical_json(m)) acts as module identity.
// Safety gating is tracked in index metadata: additive_only, consent_required.

#include <filesystem>
#include <fstream>
#include <iostream>
#include <map>
#include <set>
#include <string>
#include <vector>

#include <openssl/sha.h> // Termux: pkg install openssl openssl-dev clang

namespace fs = std::filesystem;

static std::string sha256_hex(const std::string& data) {
  unsigned char hash[SHA256_DIGEST_LENGTH];
  SHA256((const unsigned char*)data.data(), data.size(), hash);

  static const char* hex = "0123456789abcdef";
  std::string out;
  out.reserve(64);
  for (int i = 0; i < SHA256_DIGEST_LENGTH; i++) {
    out.push_back(hex[(hash[i] >> 4) & 0xF]);
    out.push_back(hex[hash[i] & 0xF]);
  }
  return out;
}

static std::string read_all(const fs::path& p) {
  std::ifstream f(p, std::ios::binary);
  return std::string((std::istreambuf_iterator<char>(f)), std::istreambuf_iterator<char>());
}

static void write_all(const fs::path& p, const std::string& s) {
  std::ofstream f(p, std::ios::binary);
  f << s;
}

int main() {
  fs::path base = "/data/data/com.termux/files/home/ghost_mast";
  fs::path jsondir = base / "processed/json";
  fs::path indexdir = base / "processed/index";
  fs::create_directories(indexdir);

  std::map<std::string, std::vector<std::string>> hash_to_files;
  std::vector<std::string> files;

  for (auto& e : fs::directory_iterator(jsondir)) {
    if (!e.is_regular_file()) continue;
    auto p = e.path();
    if (p.extension() != ".json") continue;

    std::string content = read_all(p);
    std::string h = sha256_hex(content);

    hash_to_files[h].push_back(p.filename().string());
    files.push_back(p.filename().string());
  }

  // Build a simple JSON index (without full JSON parsing).
  std::string out = "{\n  \"index_version\": \"1.0\",\n  \"generated\": true,\n";
  out += "  \"module_count\": " + std::to_string(files.size()) + ",\n";
  out += "  \"unique_hashes\": " + std::to_string(hash_to_files.size()) + ",\n";
  out += "  \"modules\": [\n";

  bool first = true;
  for (auto& [h, flist] : hash_to_files) {
    if (!first) out += ",\n";
    first = false;

    out += "    {\n";
    out += "      \"hash_sha256\": \"" + h + "\",\n";
    out += "      \"files\": [";
    for (size_t i = 0; i < flist.size(); i++) {
      out += "\"" + flist[i] + "\"";
      if (i + 1 < flist.size()) out += ", ";
    }
    out += "]\n";
    out += "    }";
  }

  out += "\n  ]\n}\n";

  fs::path index_path = indexdir / "index.json";
  write_all(index_path, out);

  std::cout << "Wrote: " << index_path << "\n";
  std::cout << "Total modules: " << files.size() << "\n";
  std::cout << "Unique hashes: " << hash_to_files.size() << "\n";
  return 0;
}pkg install -y clang openssl openssl-dev

  if grep -q "Bootstrapped 100" ~/.tor/tor.log 2>/dev/null; then
    echo "✅ Tor ready"
    break
  fi
  sleep 1
  printf "."
done
echo ""

# 5. Test Tor
TOR_IP=$(curl --socks5 127.0.0.1:9050 --socks5-hostname 127.0.0.1:9050 --max-time 10 -s https://check.torproject.org/api/ip 2>/dev/null | jq -r '.IP')
if echo "$TOR_IP" | grep -qE '^[0-9]'; then
  echo "✅ Tor works – exit IP: $TOR_IP"
else
  echo "⚠️ Tor still bootstrapping – check later: tail ~/.tor/tor.log"
fi

# 6. Launch DuckDuckGo (system‑wide VPN)
am start -n com.duckduckgo.mobile.android/.ui.main.MainActivity 2>/dev/null && echo "🦆 DuckDuckGo launched – enable VPN in app"

# 7. Create Chrome proxy switcher script (no extension needed)
cat > ~/set_chrome_proxy.sh << 'PROXYEOF'
#!/data/data/com.termux/files/usr/bin/bash
echo "To set Chrome proxy manually:"
echo "1. Open Chrome → Settings → Privacy & Security → Proxy"
echo "2. Choose 'Manual proxy configuration'"
echo "3. SOCKS host: 127.0.0.1  Port: 9050"
echo "4. SOCKS v5"
echo ""
echo "Or use a Chrome extension like 'Proxy SwitchyOmega' (auto-switch)."
PROXYEOF
chmod +x ~/set_chrome_proxy.sh

echo ""
echo "━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━"
echo "✅ SETUP COMPLETE"
echo "━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━"
echo "Tor SOCKS5   : 127.0.0.1:9050"
echo "Tor status   : $(pgrep -x tor > /dev/null && echo RUNNING || echo STOPPED)"
echo "DDG VPN      : open app & enable"
echo ""
echo "To use Tor in terminal:"
echo "  torsocks curl https://check.torproject.org/api/ip"
echo ""
echo "To set Chrome proxy manually, run:"
echo "  bash ~/set_chrome_proxy.sh"{
